2025-08-18T17:28:40.2052666Z         """Wait until feed_data() or feed_eof() is called.

2025-08-18T17:28:40.2053620Z         # StreamReader uses a future to link the protocol feed_data() method
2025-08-18T17:28:40.2054025Z         # to a read coroutine. Running two read coroutines at the same time
2025-08-18T17:28:40.2054409Z         # would have an unexpected behaviour. It would not possible to know
2025-08-18T17:28:40.2054743Z         # which coroutine would get the next data.

2025-08-18T17:28:40.2055239Z             raise RuntimeError(
2025-08-18T17:28:40.2055497Z                 f'{func_name}() called while another coroutine is '

2025-08-18T17:28:40.2056223Z     
2025-08-18T17:28:40.2056427Z         assert not self._eof, '_wait_for_data after EOF'
2025-08-18T17:28:40.2056690Z     
2025-08-18T17:28:40.2056923Z         # Waiting for data while paused will make deadlock, so prevent it.
2025-08-18T17:28:40.2057327Z         # This is essential for readexactly(n) for case when n > self._limit.
